ethyopiens cryspe corled whiche combed ten tymes daye hathe theyr habytes shorte one maye almoost se theyr ar haue theyr neckes charged grete chaynes ben replenysshed golden jewelles theyr handes full bordred wt veluet wt sylke clokes bended dyuers colour dyuers clothes worne present tyme gownes haue double rebraced colers theyr shertes ben fronced golde sylke ye fynest clothe yt founden guyse infideles turkes sarazyns vyle abhomynable grete shone rounde boule squared buskynges cut slyppers bygared hosen garded bended veluet satyn purse sachelles gyrdylles taffeta lacketh nothynge saue fayre swerde hanger theyr syde crystendome crystendome yf thou haue mortalytes epydemees thou arte cause therof saye notefye yt yu haste endured suche habytes haue ben worne worse yet worne thou shalt haue yet dyuers punycyons yf shorte tyme thou remedy cast awaye newe guy customes aswel men woman vyle dyshonest mayst thou well thynke sauyour worlde shall juge ye humaynes mysdedes wyll reuenge hy p auncyent fooles ca v p ala euer enclyne sepulture bothe houre daye yet leue folysshe ruyne haue contynued alwaye olde fooles euer hathe kepte laye wherfore olde fooles maye chefe vyce hathe ben lefe awaken spyrytes auncyent folkes whiche haue ben fooles lyfe herken olde foole maketh co playnte grete foly ryght vycyous replenysshed bytternes hath euer remayned syth myn enfancye may suffre leue myne auncyent custome fyrste lyfe chylde yet ye maye se go haue c yere yet wyser wonte almoost prudent wyse byrthe worse wolde wyser sygnes token fooles shewe mynyster chyldren wryte folysshe regyme foly haue made testament whiche conteyneth techeth doctryne vnto wyll folowe lyue folysshely haue done ryght euyll luna esaye xvi tyke conductour leder fooles haue ensued folowed doctryne toure vyces euyll example whiche lerned shewe nowe experyence myn innocent dedes c ex sludits specyfyeth foole foly desyre haue louynge praysynge euery place whereas go may well gyue knowlege haue sowen euyll renowne dyuers place countres c cum tu te de presum folyshnes vyle demonstraunce vyce synne foly dyshonour thynketh grete honoure mlegyos euylles hathe ben sowen vpon erth haue herte ryght sorowfull maye oo haue grete dyspyre may consume clothes vnto ende none myght syth olde auncyent may regne wyll lerne chyldren neuewes haue done faynynge vyces waye ryght ample euery place lo fader gyueth euyll example vnto chyldren neuewes whiche becometh vycyous peruers halfe fader whiche gretely reioysed wolde ryght angrye saye chyldren benygne dule melancoly chyldren shall fynysshe de consecra ti di v c vl glosa theyr lyues sythe lyue soo vycyously wherfore saye worthy gouerne oure shyp whan cometh ony tormente ala olde foole wherfore hast thou shame yt thy foly hathe surmounted longe hast thou remors conscyence lyue longe vyle synne abhomynable knowest yu euyll whiche rooted taken awaye afterwarde whan one abydeth longe daniel xiiii remedye cause grete payne may detray meurs ben roted herte p documente chyldren ca vi p forgyueth crymes ryght vycyous chyldren withouten correctynge enduceth vertues gloryous well worthy haue grete tormentynge anguysshe longe contynuynge seketh wayes lyue sorowe folysshe man yonge chyldren whiche desyreth lyue well ryghtwysly reste herken doctrynes also faders haue chyldren puyssaunce fader shall alwaye myserable gretely affusked hathe aspecte vnto chyldren dothe payne solycytude reduce vnto vertuous operacions ferynge dethe cometh vpon theyr werkes vnresonable mortall also fole detestable manyfest seeth chyldren euyll careth therfore ala well consydered suffre youthe voluptuous renne euery withouten conductour gouernoure whan flocke shepe ben without pastour leue theyr hye waye errynge strayenge feldes playnes suche wyse oftentymes wulfe cometh deuoureth lyke wyse yonge chyldren resorteth vnto vycyous place dothe comprehende well p folysshe fader vnreasonable dombe beest whan one accuseth chyldren trespace excuseth saynge youthe haue reason know whether doo well euyll poore fooles well theyr youthe excuse knowest thou thou blynde fader sapyence groweth tender meurs dysposeth ye lycoure doctryne holy lyfe knowest thou sapyence adresseth sooner vnto yonge folkes vnto olde retayne better theyr vnder stondyng ben fallen aege orace sayth one take newe erthen pot put swete smel oracius lynge floures therin shall smell euer loures ye put stynkynge thynge shall haue euer stynkynge odoure take ensample also yonge tree one maye bowe eche manere wyse whan tree grete stronge one maye bowe without brekynge wherfore faders endoctryne chyldren theyr florysshynge youthe retably swete correccyon dyscyplyne enduceth yon ge chyldre vnto vertues causeth eschewe vyces rede kynge pryam accorded vnto ye priamus troyanus wyll chyldren wherfore grete cyte troye oppressed grekes fynably kynge pryam sawe cyte destroyed thrughe consentynge wyll parys grece auys hed brought awaye fayre helayne ouer haue paris elena another example proude tarquyn ye kynges sone rome rauysshed fayre lucrece whiche tarqu u filius tarquy ni superbi regis romano u de quo va lerius mors luciane latellina pure sorowe slewe herselfe frendes happened afterwarde bothe fader chased rome vylaynously bycause neuer kynge rome syth wryten also catellyna dyuers cruell per er hym neuewes became cruell vyllaynous dedes homycyde theyr vncle ben afore thrughe vycyous example fader hathe ben euyll chyld shall vycyous moost comynly chy e ensueth fader wherfore saye better chyl de ensue good prudent men folowe grete company fooles replete vyces fynde also kynge peleus resplendysshynge peleus achilles worlde gaue phenyxe vnto achylles endoctryne teche good vertues phenyxe dyscrete ruayllous thynge se lyke wyse dyde kynge phylyppe florysshyng philippus alexander worlde gaue sone alexaunder vnto arystotle prynce phylosophres hadde comprehended al documentes platon instructe chylde alexa der well scyence kynge worlde dyscrete fader good mayster gracyous dyscyple presente tyme soo nowe holden reputed shame folysshe faders setteth store set theyr chyldren ole lerne scyence floure worldly thynges complayneth theyr expences therfore frome folysshe fader yssueth folysshe chyldren full ygn rau e folysshe redotyn f der well content e chyldren dy end g de vyces excesse vyllaynously dysprayse good vertues ope aristot e plato racyons thynke vpon harde complaynt crate made whan sayd thus yf amytted speke wolde name fooles redotynge yt assembleth pecunes treasours dysceytes fallacious chyldren successours yt afterwarde shall spende excesse vyle superfluytes ala poore faders ye leue chyldren vnpuruayed ygnoraut scyence folysshe bestyall lunatykes whiche thynge ye shall repente faders full sore afterwarde whan ye shall bytten dyuers morsures bycause ye chastysed endoctryned good operacyons condycyons vycyous dyspraysynge thynges dyuine ben wycked euyll lyfe haue theyr spyrytes rauysshed dyspryseth treasours yt theyr fader hathe assembled fyxeth theyr herte prouerb x rate anus mynde vyle synne lecherye yt ardaunt fyre burneth resplendysshynge floure youthe drynky ge wyne insacyately etynge excessyue mete yonge chyldren yt nourysshed doctryne aege nothynge dygne memorye faders knowe yt nothynge better nourysshe chyldren prouerb xix ecclia xxii make florysshe vertues good doctrine begynnynge myddel ende shal good grete thinge noblesse pucelles ben therwith decored prouffyteth noblesse vnto deutere xxi hathe acquyred payue laboure yt replenysshed vertues excellent prudence good condycyons al decored aourned vyle abhomynable vyces wherfore presume noblesse yt haue deserued due payne poftentymes mylde bytche bryngeth forth shrewed seneca juuenalis whelpes lyke wyse good moders hathe ryght vycyous chyldren yf chyldren dyuers fader culpable theyr vycyousnes yf correcte ecc xxii theyr youthe yf fader chastyse coulpe pof reportours detractours ca vii pwho maketh debate also stryfe false enuy double retortynge whiche synfully ledeth lyfe euer vyce synne contynuynge without remors inwarde repentynge bytwene two mylstones body dothe bere haue guerdon ye may se amonge flaterers cause prouer xvi euylles prynte well mynde hertes doctryne whiche thynketh supported wt makynge lye dyscordes lyfe naturall foole shall neuer prospere goodnes makynge dyscencyons bytwene true louers false reportynge bytwene man man butshall fynysshe day wretchedly false detraccyon hathe caused many inconuenyentes fall dyuers regyons dayly dothe hathe mouthe full venym wherwith sleeth good renowne dyuers good persones tongue full lye redy saw fraudes dyscencyons betwene true louers felowes oftentymes castyge forthe vayne wordes courage poore innocentes ben wounded dymynysshynge theyr enuyes vertuous condycyons desyrynge whiche good concorde pea maye debate dyscorde euyl reporter oftentymes accuseth good uerb xxix et xxiiii folkes knowe whens cometh vnto malycyous tongue shall happen many dolour anguysshes tormentes soweth vyciously dyscordes amonge true louers neyghbours tell worse false reportour detra tour veretably nothynge vnder esperyes heuen nothynge vyle dyshonest horryble tempest daugerous mouth yssueth wordes cautellous soo venymous maketh mortal woundes knowe two true louer two men good concorde shall neuer haue joye herte vnto tyme haue dyscencyon betwene fooles mortelles wh che xxxii vnder vmbre amyte maketh debate stryf betwene two louers thrughe false reporte detraccyon whan falsnes openly knowen ye excuse affermynge grete othes ye causer debate ye neuer sayd thynge touchynge theyr dyshonoure soo false reporte dyssymylacyon ye holde true louers dyscencyon euer flaterynge ye kepe vp fallacyous detractours reportours full malyce enuye yt procureth daye daye noyses debate euery place tongue serpentine venymeth worlde cursed folke whome yssueth dole anguysshe ye worthy lyue ye breke good alyaunce ye ought put dure aspre pryson remayne euer without lyght ye prouerb xix worthy haue lyght lyfe ensueth good counsayll capitulo ix phe reputed naturall foole nothynge dyscerne ceason werkes wente scoole grounded reason yet may happen encheason whan ploweth full dyshonoure bycause wyll counterfet hymselfe shewe hymself dyscrete well knowynge cautell prudent euer thynge maynteyned folyssher th whiche haue theyr vnderstondynge persecuted cautellous euer eenee also wyse salam xiiii xi also eloquent tullyus also stronge sampson dyscrete duyde also pacyent job also merc full danyell also fayre absolon yet yf prouerb ecclesia xix entached presumpcyon ye fooles sh dysprayseth wyse mennes counsayll good oppynyons myght reuoke wytte enforce c ne fuitaris ex de con actes dyuers whiche wolde wyn honour bruyte shewynge themselfe amonge dyscrete men also compassyon bycause maynteyned kepte wyfe lyke wyse yf troyens byleued troia hector achilles nero thobias prudent men done theyr counsayll ye grekes dyspoyled brente noble cyte troye harde aduersyte se noble cyte burne yf hector wolde haue byleued fader stroke spere achilles gaue hym wherof deyed losse domage se noble valyaunt puyssaunt knyght deye moreouer cruell neron soo peruers cruell dysprysed counsayll wyse men wherfore lyke inhumayne creature slewe hymself propre handes haue also thobye ye whiche charged sone yf wolde suffre grete aduersyte sholde euer ensue documente wyse prudente men yet ouer fynde roboam kynge salamons sone wolde roboam gyue credence vnto faders seruauntes au cyent men moche dyscrete byleued complyces counsayll yonge frayle redy vyces wherin dyde wysely loste therby halfe realme fader succeded hym whiche grete shame dyshonour vnto hym also myght recounte vnto dyuers newe example yt hathe ben done oure tyme presente tyme many grete prynces wyll byleue ye cou sayll wyse dyscrete men gyueth soner crede regu xii eccl xiviii ce vnto grete sorte lusty galauntes wolde flee without wynges theyr busshes ben curyously decked whiche ben ruled gouerned theyr approche nere vnto chapytre ye shall se dyuerse thinges vtyle prouffytable helthe soules withdrawe oute shyppe foles yf ye entred therin foysshe wanhope prudente wyse men hateth vyce gretely amonge fole thou seeth wel ynoughe yf thou slepe afore thy fete mouynge gylted doctrynes fayth lawes olde antyquyte tryumphes lorde thynkest thou thyn ygnoraunce shall excuse thyn erroures shall cause plonged infernal pytte dampned syth euery body studyeth lyue vycyously maye well perceyue de cogna spiri c cum vir anti god almyghty whiche jugeth wycked cruell wyll amende theyr lyues transytory mortall worlde shall gyue horryble tormentes helle shall remayne euerlastynge payne without seynge ony lyght daye euer create ecclesia iii p fooles vnpuruayed ca xii fastneth sadle well upon horse whan shall ryde unto towne stuffe sell thynkynge sure euery syde yf falle dytche syde passe maye hym saye lyeth foole without delaye awake spyrytes fooles vnpuruayed yt alway slombrynge thynges transytory remembreth felycyte thy soule uerb xiiii cause knowe many dyuers fooles worlde errynge fro way veryte haue grete wyll reduce vnto hye waye ye ende adnychyll theyr insacyate erroures ryght daungerous ygnoraunt vnpuruayed wytte reason neuer thynketh thynges come yf aduenture come ony fortune hym wyll saye ala thought suche fortune sholde haue befallen whan seneca fortune passed studye myght eschewe ye ende yt appese theyr sorowe e must al waye thynke tyme present tyme future eccle xxxiii well wyse man seeth thynges come foole full vnpurueyauce shytteth stable dore whan horse stolen hathe vnderstondynge ryghte good puruayeth hym tyme come maye eschewe daungers peryllous shall sure season prouydynge tyme future yf adam taken regarde vnto dyshonoure salustius adam eua shame happened hym eue eten forboden fruyte lorde wolde neuer haue dryuen paradyse terrestre auncyent faders ben dy sceased haue wepte theyr synnes ye space many yeres lyke wyse yf jonathas hadde byleued triphon whan arryued jonathas mach abeorum xii bethsan hadde thought myshappe propre seruaunt habandoned hym goodes whiche jonathas toke grete gyftes yf lefte grete multytude folke ben vnder coloure dethe incontynente place rede also cayn slewe owne broder eccl xlviii enuye haue ensample semblably atreus whome broder occupyed parke well realme stronge puyssaunt defende lanus theseus expulsed bloode horrour se two chyldren ye dyscrete lyke wyse ethyocles bredern receyued grete enormytees cursed enuye thou prudent man yf thou wylte dyscrete good wyse fle enuye thou shalte fynde thyselfe ymagynynge wrathe agaynste hym wyll brewe daungerous drynke make hym put darke pryson saynge hathe iniuryed ye kynges persone euyll reporte yt hathe stolen thynge murdred wyll pretende make hym slayne whan set appereth medea detrenched two chyldren yt medea de q seneca dea made jason vncle deye p progne dyde worse bycause wolde auenged vpon husbande tereus progne de q ouidius vi meth vyoled syster cut systers tongue called phylomyna slewe sone whiche grete cruelte made hym soden boyled rosted gaue tereus hym ete juuenall whiche dyscrete man hathe sayd moche euyll woman ouyde dyuerse take well hauynge dolour herselfe comynge agaynst holy fayth well faculte loue accompanyed husbande abusyon leest theyr two hertes conioyned togyder one dyfferente wyl juuenalis uer xxx go stately gorgyously apperteyneth juuenalis fourthe susteyned fyrst seruaunt becometh mayster seconde seruaute alwaye dronke thyrde wyfe furyous full debate fourthe mayden full pryde herytour lady maystresse suche mayden thou ought eschewe flee gyueth oftentymes drynke drynke wherin reposeth venym conclusyon euer beware femynyne gendre reuolue myndes cursydnes agrypyne shal specefye vnto agrippina pontia danaides danaydes fyfty systers maryed whiche comyn assente slewe theyr husbandes fyrst nyght theyr maryage saue one vertuous ynoughe ala lucresse arte thou gone lucretia thou wolde nothynge haue maculed thyn honoure fewe nowe dayes bounden wt thy chastyte lyke wyse many yt holdeth thy courage soner place wayes sene thades hepes lubryke swyne chaste ryghte thays thynly sowen cathon thou happy haue founden wyse porcya thou agamenon portia ca vnhappy haue founde clytemestra euery body wolde clitemestra fayne fynde sabyna happeneth oftentymes sabina man fyndeth euyll wyfe meane ye whiche assured happy yt fyndeth wyse wyfe uer xii eccl xxv et xxvi dyscrete well dysposed kepe fayth trouthe husbande suche wyues worthy put cronycles p puyssaunce fooles ca lxii p fooles saye haue puyssaunce bycause theyr superbyous fole wenest thou possede many scyences bycause thy rente herytages naye thou sapien v uer xvii et xxiiii eccle xxxiii p ix uer xxvii eccle xv xxii q ii pri resembleth vnto blynde man relacyon ony thynge taketh ye job xxxvii uer xx tyme cometh ryche pore abasshed thus replenysshed vertues kepeth realme ecclesia x sapien vi pea vnyon londe yonge kyge prynce wel assured gouerne eccle v x uer xxx sapien xi dyscretely counsayllers entendeth saue ete drynke nocturnally diurtenes gaudeamus londes goodes dyssypered ecclesia x foole set syege inherte mynystre euery body justyce equyte whiche justyce yssueth ryght tourneth lawes ye volente euyll persone maketh lyght jugementes yf haue gode frendes partye symplenesse wel adnychyl sapi vi xii led ryghtes ought egally maynteyned wherin wherthorughe thou loste thy skynne thy lute example hym dyuers fooles soo obstynate thynkynge themselfe ryght wyse prudente wyll vsurpe se ryed wt theyr obstynacyes mockeryes whiche apperceyue wel neuerthelesse fooles thyn ke playe yf se purpense many fraudes detraccyons flateryes wyll byleue true yf ye wyll knowe suche folkes haue sygne foly theyr hedes thou haste ben ryche thou haste yet thy coffres full rychesses doubte thou shalt haue kynnes men frendes felowes ynoughe whan thy rychesse gone thou shalte neuer haue frende kynne poore man hathe frendes p spende thy goodes playes none dysportes yu modygalytees thenne wyll good men flee whan thou haste dyspended thy goodes whiche thy truste rychesse shal leue pouerte wyll ssayll euery body shall blame thou wylte cquyre frende recouer thy hasarde hall late thou goodes ynoughe thy lyfe haue socoured thy frende thou haste despended consumed shorte tyme thou arte fole u alime rn ff vbi pup edu deb thou shalte fynde none amyte vyces ye whiche vyle abhomynable wolde men sholde saye halfe reproches saye vnto wolde madde play otherwyse praye yt thou speke auenture whan worde departed mouthe subiectes vnto sayd wordes hathe rest renneth alwaye whan oute moost strongest worlde retraye agayne thynke yt thy tongue speke daungerous wordes wynne vertues beholde thyn exemplayre whiche thyn ge ought done neuer vnto another yt whiche thou wolde dyde vnto yf thou wylte put ye thy sacke beholde grete euyll thy mouthe bereth hurte poore foole beholde thy speche ende thou dyffame thy neyghboure tentymes make pytte folkes falleth therin themselfe fyrste amon done dyuers euyl le vnto mardocheus whiche wyse man prudente notwithstondynge made crosse hym patybulayre gybet aman cautelles vnhappynes fell therin hanged without ony respyte behoueth euery case consyder chose good meane leuynge detraccyons decepcyons dyssymulacyons fraudes extorcyons dothe well putteth affyauce bycause maketh taste bytter droppe promesses truste maye one apperceyue syght man hathe good fayth hym one knowe thou lodge hathe enuy vpon praye ye answere hym wysely thou neuer wyse thou knowe hys secretes hese host thy pleasure ete drynke hardely house haue fere haue ony hurte thou arte foole ete thy fyll thou knowe socoure ende thou deceyued eschewehy laugheth mockynge desyreth thy dethe p vnpurueynge tyme come ca lxviii p hongre atteyneth hym vyle chaunce neuer thynketh tyme come passeth yongthe transytory thynges folysshe dysportes grete inco uenyence ala yes meschaunt sholde haue aspecte vnto yf shall assemble goodes doo oftentymes must sell londes goodes lyue ende becometh myserable also whiche maketh noo prouysyon goodes somer shall haue grete necessyte wynter extreme pouerte myserye wherfore praye take ensample pysmyres yt gadereth somer lyue wynter hony bee dothe soo lyke wyse meanes perysshe hongre frostye wynter p lytygans pleader iugement ca lxix p hathe aspecte dame justyce makynge complayntes dolorous whiche maketh grete tumulte dame justyce ye shall knowe fole maketh tumulte dame di prin justyce cryers justyce worthy punysshed greuous payne merytoryous dede maketh perturbacyon consystorye theyr jacobi iiii dyssymulacyons well cause lytell yet wyll make grete processe thyn kynge haue vengeaunce theyr fyers courage ye wene corrumpte fayre tytles lawes chapytres dame justyce ryght iocunde pleade suche folkes knowe almoost moche ye lawyer bycause go often lawe make uerbi xvii hieremie ii theyr cause kepte longe hande pleade yet knowe theyr quarell juste pretendynge corrumpte destroye ye sacred lawes uer xxvi esaye iviii decretes customed establysshed worse eschewe moche maye banysshe man bycause yt subterfuge thre dyctes sowne trompette ought called foole elles cyted ye offycyall wyl eccle xxviii eccle viii let hymselfe cursed deiecte frome prayer holy chirche careth none absolucyon wyll let hymselfe condempned iuge wyll reyse processe enuye kepe longe vp cauyllacyons fraudes agaynst ryght enryche aduocates procurours whan uee iii theyr money faylled borowe vsurye vnto tyme theyr processe fynysshed dyspoyleth hymselfe propre goodes wyll vse cautelles thynketh grete somme moneye corrumpte ye justyces ryghtes sayd folysshe aduocate wyll crye consystorye cautell haue moneye whiche shall gyuen hym subtyll vnderstondynge wyll affuske ryghte dyuers thynges whiche deporte spekynge bycause byleue suche thynges done aduocate aduerse partye may answere juge jugeth hymselfe cou sayll god aduocate sholde called p fooles abhomynable wordes ca lxx p vayne wordes dysordynate foule vnclene abhomynable reported fooles approbate peruers vnreasonable beynge therin insacyable deseruynge maladyccyons brekynge good constytucyons inutyle fooles whiche applyeth yourselfe vyle dishonest wordes come se ecclesi li esdre vi mathei v corin xv xxviii q se pe purpose ye shall lerne speke honestlye dyuers foles named gorbyens ben assembled togyder grete hepes halowynge festes theyr auncyent faders loue thynges enorme well men woman enhaunce aulters theyr faders whan haue vysyted ye chirches olde yonge man woman vyrgyn mayden chaste without ony ordre renneth medleth abhomynacyons makynge feest berynge ensence theyr handes spekynge vyle wordes makynge grete noyse tumulte one chastyse syne synne holdeth alwayes reygne erthe without vertues haue shame vyr gynyte due pouerte re de quo herodo li uer xii eccle xvi marti x wherfore loue otherthynge myrre ourselfe vnhappy moneye ledeth soule vnto helle tell auaylled rychesse vnto kynge crassus sardanapal speke shortly condycyons wyll goo waye josue vii uer xxvi exodi xvi nume xiiii veryte justyce ryght whan halfe waye torne brydell ye waye polluted strayeth ye ryght waye tourne theyr face awaye beholde perfounde euyll departe goodes whiche loued well thou takest euery body kynge duke erle thou goth frely knocketh theyr gate without beholdynge wherfore thy courage fyerse one wolde gyue grete somme moneye thou wolde haue dysdayne yet yf pope ye rustyke procure thou wylt nothynge thou wylte beholde none euyll tyme shortely wyll destroye yf reygned domyned euer worlde syth nestreus vntyll presente tyme syth thou yt without hauynge goodes fader moder thou arte bounden nourysshe ye ryght wryten elles thou puttest thy soule grete daunger ye scrypture sayeth peruers chyldren ben worthy put fyre hell thynke crystyens dysprayse god euery day yf chase jewes countrees knowe entencyon ende entende certaynly vsurye alonely vnto jewes thus without vertues expulsed god holy crysten men vndyscrete paccyon spere sharper stele vnto crysten brederen horryble wulues famysshed holdeth poore shepe auaryce commyt vsurye fraudulously xiiii q iiii nec hoc et c se et c quicun que enraged grete hete desyre derthenes ben sene dyuers hanged quartred yf ye sholde haue punysshement ye ought euer saye trouthe wyse man neuer fereth payne fauoure kepeth stedfaste fotynge agaynst euery body vertue fauoureth hym co tente correccyon euer replete scyence repreueth synners theyr vyces reduseth vnto vertuous ue ix luce vii ecc xxxvi eccle xxi hiere li lyuynge thynke saynt johan baptyst whiche replenysshed holynes ensued vertues fledde vyces holynes good lyfe god humylyed hym vnto hym praynge hym bapty sehym fayned hym correcke herode antypas bycause helde wyfe herodiades whiche broder herode antypas pcorrecke theyr vyces synnes swete wordes yf receyue correccyon yet shall receyue meryte one waye ye repreuynge synne correckynge thy good dede shall loste worldly thynges hyde trouthe letteth saye trouthe gyftes dampneth soule truely whan doctours ben bysshoppes haue benefyces ye shall preche crye trouthe hydde may take ye payne syde dare saye nothynge lest sholde lese theyr benefyces withdrawe good dede ca c p wyll let man prudent werkes honeste put ony empesshemente betwene folke affynyte foole certaynte thynkynge let good dede whiche may spede partes assemble fooles whiche thynketh withdrawe good dedes math xvi marti viii uer xxiiii ad rom p xxxvi grete foly come rede scryptu ye shall fynde thynges ryght prouffytable helthe soules foole full wanhope whiche thynketh lette good operacyons impetuous full crudelyte taketh handes haue intellygence saynges wyll saye iust man rchersynge good purpose shall argued ye foole hathe iuche wyll wyll euery body accorde vnto hym hondreth wylspeke yf ony wylde reason luce xii thimo iiii mathei v ii thimo ii wytte wyll lyue secretely lyke vnreasonable foole vyle thynges mondayne pleaseth hym dysprayseth god wanhope grete foly makynge ypocryte begylynge symple folkes maketh ypocryte wherby wyse men deceyued wylles semblable vnto foole c vi vii xxiiii q c se luce xxii uer xiiii eccle xxxvii hiere xix ad co iii suffre none aduersyte wyse man dothe prospere goodnes vertues p obmyssyon good werkes ca c ii p whiche hathe lampe replete oyle may better se also hathe vertues grete accomplyssheth truele lyueth grete prosperyte whiche dothe lyue well yf thou perseuer vnto ye ende thou lesest thy tyme ende crowneth god ryghtwys juge wyll iuge euery mortall man houre fyndeth hym good withoute takynge respyte whan cometh dethe shall call shall make coueytynge haue hyghe tytles hyghe name true degre sapyence one neuer excellent tytle vsurpeth name magystrall hadde neuer scyence ambycyous gothe taketh ensygne teche people haue praysynge ende say wyse engendreth vycyousnes aduyse vnto wyll entende ende dyuerse banquette feestes somoned fyrste lyke wyse grete assembles bycause haue tytle without scyence wryten yt scyence god fader aboue heuen scyence tell haue none worlde whiche founde v hym accomplysshed scyence abdie mo corinth esaye judith vii actuu xii foly dyuers present tyme ye worlde theyr grete profounde studye haue abour payne waye tyll dethe hym take without delaye impeteous fooles vnfortuned whiche setteth noughte mysfortunes come rede chapytre ye shall se mysfortune euery body thynkynge affayres fayth garnysshed knowe ye descendynge therof vnstablenes se worldly thynges sure whiche thynketh happye falle incontynente fortune ben sodayne hande neuer stronge may go agaynst nothynge worlde taketh ende ye whiche haue thought mynde haue stablenes whome fortune agreable well cometh socoure theyr ruyne alway applyaunt vnto vnnaturell good prest redy doo euyll foole fyndeth hymselfe house fyre goodes consumed thou man yf thou haue vnfortune hiere li ezech xxvi ff como l si vt uer vii thy heed well combed brede lyce vermyne prudentes saye comyn prouerbe come yll neuer alone faute encreaseth se euery daye fortune encreaseth v dede greuous yt worthy recyted notwithstondynge thynke transmutacy ons contempled many thynges cometh v happeneth oftentymes one thynketh ende man withoute dothe well kepeth hymselfe euyll whan knoweth eccle lxiii uer xxiii luce vii eccle si iii esaye xxiii job iiii sapien xiiii shoulde kepe hym dothe haue one fote surely one must loke setteth oftentymes fortune hydeth vnder fote man euen man wyll go vpon se waxeth swel leth wherfore foole entreth shyppe may susteyne wawes alytell wynde whiche oftentymes peryssheth thrughe haboundau ce tempeste orage thus foole receyueth grete domage dyuers tymes thrughe folyshnes bycause gouerne wyse man kepeth hym daungers aforesayd eschewynge orages se maye happen wherfore euery body thynketh go vpon se ought haue sure stronge shyppe ende maye resyste agaynst wawes tempestes wherfore synners consyder vnfortunes worlde amende lyues ende ye well fortuned realme paradyse p detraccyon goodes ca c v p wyse man lyueth well without fraude detraccyon afterwarde hangeth bell cattes necke correccyon foole without dyscrecyon last condyscende unto foly make ende amonge fooles adnychylleth go de vndyscrecyons come rede chapytre ye shall fynde thynges prouffytable soules dyscrete wyse prudente men haue volente well delyted theyr puyssaunce bycause grete congregacyon fooles regystred booke whiche haue put grete shyppe foure toppes haue barge rowynge vppon se dyuers nacyons wyll wryte theyr detraccyons renownes speke malefactours peruers ful iniquyte ende sholde amende theym good men sholde reioyse maynteyne bounte whiche iii dis deni que esaie xxviiii xliiii dis c ff deori iu l math xv actuu vi xliiii dis reuerentia fallacyous deceyuours auarycyous men replete enormytees dyssolate table insacyable etynge without shame drynke without remyssyon swaloweth morselles hole hast theyr trenchours laden lyke mountioyes theyr cuppes full wyne ale whan haue dyned ryse ye table without gyuynge ony thankes vnto god goodes vyle abhomynable table haue grete horrour recounte drynke tyll theyr eye watre theyr tethe rotten drynke haue dronken yeske boke vome mou de con dis v omnibus plinius li xiiii circa fi c crapula de vi ho hora epi persius de reli san c xxxv dis lux receyue drynkes prouoke one theyr house drynke excessyfly ouercometh theyr stomackes drynke vnto theyr god bacchus one vnto cuppes pottes full enforcynge xxxvii tulli seneca juuenalis yonge wyllsytte aboue olde ete delycyous mete without ony shame burgeyse marchaunt put themselfe euer platter drynke etynge theyr potage consume theyr vyllaynous handes wyl touche mete wyll blowe theyr nose without ony mesure wyll ete theyr mete wyll drynke without makynge clene theyr mouthes synge dysplayed throtes makyng many vyle sacrefyces god bacchus breke pottes glass platter dysshes saucer hurly ge vpon erthe men enraged naturall wyttes drynkynge tyme ete whiche seruauntes sholde ete sardana palus thou hast dyuers companyons worlde wyll put glotons werke haue fourme lyue honestly well ye one grece latyns hebrewes eche hathe maner lyue one fatte lene ye maner theyr countrees symple gracyous honest vertuous wyse dronkertes glotons haue eten dronken moche theyr belyes aketh demaunde ye realme paradyse haue theyr thought superfluous thynke go paradyse maner ala ihesus thou haste made v drynke wyne ete mete worlde also thou hast comaunded v yt glotons take repast moderately ala bodyes fumeth haboundaunce mete haue truste stronge drynkynge lyues shall prolonged lyke wyse wyne wyll make v haue good blode also soules vpholden blode al god sayeth hathe ordeyned mesure tyme houre ete drynke excessyfe consumeth body soule abredgeth lyfe vertues somtyme noblenesse courtes prynces nowe present tyme astonyed gese corrumped dronke ne pompes estate ful flateryes haue lost name auncyent men renowmed vndyscrete men werkes auncyent men appety teth holy lawes haue wryten dyuers bookes nowe knowe nothynge wylde beestes scyence gouerned pore vertuous men eleuate honour oftentymes preferred afore noblenesse p foles dysfygured takynge straunge clothynges ca c vii p democrytus sapyent sawe grete foly fooles neclygent laughed faste hye bycause coude polycye cynycus wepeth ryght fast bycause worlde stedfast yf demochrytus lyued sawe many fooles worlde wolde laughe crassus wolde laughe also se enormytees mondayne fooles ye whiche uer xiiii juuenalis l si c de pe plini li vii solinus crassus de vi ho cle cu decore neuer wyll laughe one wherfore auncyent phylosophers haue wylled wryte stondynge wolde laughe ye obscure tempestes se fooles garded bordred dysfygured whiche full vyces synnes weneth iuste one may knowe rese ble preestes god mar whiche wyll doo sacrefyce grete furoure apparaylleth doo vyle sacrefyce remeuynge theyr bodyes manere daunce fooles bere vesture symulacre druyde de quib lucan menades persi sati resemble chymere one wayleth wepeth bycause wolde appere fayre anoyteth hym swete oyntemetes ye one hathe vysage mortefyed olde bere vesture lusty galant haue euer borowed clothes haue party clothes haue theyr gownes getyque thus make theyr pompes couterfetteth deuylles vysage ferefull abhomynable louer bereth lemures de quibus duo eccle xxv c de epi c l mime ant de san epi col ix saturnalia copitalitia mamurius instrument musyque playnge swetely ende yonge maydens may afore dore burgeyse wyfe rennynge vpon nyght lesynge theyr tyme vycyously mayden reioyseth thynkynge decepcyons corrumpeth hertes tendre maydens lycoure vyrgynall theyr softe beddes dyssolucyons done worlde thrughe vyle synners shall come thy house stele thy hennes fleeth suche folke shall comytte innumerable synnes incessauntly noyses debate cryes exclamacyons represent make feest saturne men theyr wyttes goynge peruers hertes crabbed ape hydynge theyr vysages hydeous face resembleth almoost dethe theyr bodyes couered vyle vesture faber c de pe l si quis de cri fal ad audi entiam fucare peruers fooles wyll chaunge nature corporall otherwyse god hathe gyuen wyll redresse immaculacyon humanyte se vanyte forme shall affusked alonely vnto suche folkes burgeyses full rychesses co playne symulacres deceptyues holy feestes place serue god vyrgyn mary daunces lecherye playes without obseruynge ye holy feestes ony wyse tyme lente whan euery body sholde haue benedyccyon god take false vysages pleasure full vyces whiche lye alwayes yf ryse late perseuer vnto ende yf come ony correcke v set nought therby synne ashamed knowe well maculacyon maye take correccyon ala correccyon whether gone nowe thynne sowen crystendo de con dis v quadragesia euery doth nature ryght oughte iniuryes vnto theym wereth habyte deuylles certaynly shall bere vnto hell laste p true descrypcyon prudent men ca c viii p wyse man whiche prudent dothe moche good euer go gyuynge example excellent unto whiche wo techynge vertues may synne fall yf hertly god call come good doctryne foles yt knoweth prudence ye shall dyscrypcyon prudent man ensygnemetes socrates uirgilius neca e pi qudec tu uyrgyle socrates haue ben autentyques sayd vnyuersall worlde none foude seblables scyence wher fore thynketh dygne haue degre theyr souerayne louynge socrates grece uyrgyll sayeth verse dyuyne scyence wysdome hanged hym vertue bounte made hym refulgent juge careth chydynges ecclesia sapien cryenges people wyse yssueth grete lyght justyce noysom equyte euer ye ryght waye wyll slepe daye tyll haue thought whiche necessarye hym wyse men euery houre replete grete vertues grete praysynges bereth semblaunce aungelles ihesus wyll wolde yt ecclesi vi uer x eccle xviii ecclesi xii ec xxxviii ecclesia uer iiii esay v uer xxix aristides lurias fabricus plato latho uer ix sapien v germanie defectu euery body resplendysshed scyence euery bodyes conscyence clene grete meruayll yf many foles present tyme vary grete lady scyence yonge courage haue sapyence trauayll shall abyde without hauyng ony goodes begylers full fraudes malyces wyll saye haue iuste tytle noblenes yf knewe nothynge ala aristides iuste noble curius good fabricus souerayne plato grete cathon shall haue nowe preemynence tyme dame sapyence regned bycause fooles nothynge whiche mocketh wyse men gyuen monday ne glorye honour prayse haue grete auau tages well indygne whome grete robberyes fraudes adressed vsurpe place whiche ordeyned wyse dyscrete men whiche haue better deserued almay ne vyctoryous gyuen rewardes vnto euery body renowne ben soo moche dymynysshed sholde haue ben many fooles shyppe wyll applye holy scyence kepe holy comaundementes god folysshe vesture full myseryes haue wryten put fygure foole wyll lyue wysely also longe reygneth worlde lyue wrytynge uyrgyle knowe shall haue shorte tyme good dedes rest heuen perdurably kepe thy body thy soule amende ende thou maye tast herbe called ambrosia folkes replete foly come wysedome sayeth taste worthy pasture offre chyldren vnto sapyence pryncypall lady ende ye may haue dyscrecyon kynges somtyme sapyence tyme uer xiii uirgilius ecclesia iii sapien vi titio theba qui et brant haue theyr dysporte vanytees defyle holy scryptures alexandre ye grete soo well lerned made cronycles hymselfe latyn fayre rethoryke made nothynge whiche iuste done hym men armes p recomendacyon phylosophye ca cix p tyme doctryne decayed nought set place euery man well appayed gete good grete solace carynge space puttynge fayre dygne sophye fete phylosophye awaken lytell spyrytes entendeth vnto thynges superiours someuer dothe pretende without p xix johelis apoca vi sap n tu archi oporta ecclesia iii uer ii ecclesi purpose wyl ascende hye foole sholde ymagyne pretende yf clene membres ende hyghe sacrefyces encence apperteyneth vnto phylosophye endued ensygnementes refulgente dyuyne acquayntaunce eloquence swete pleasaunt solace vayne desyres inutyle documentes good lyuynge ensue holynes swete sure waye paradyse ala may put euylles behynde eschewe vyle vyces haue alegement god hymselfe hathe sente v worlde lyue well also whan shall haue nede sapyence vertues maye mynystre vnto v extremytees demaunde hym good herte intere wyll hym receptacle ye poore gendre humayne whiche prepared fayre ornementes gyrded vesture people clothe fyne sendall aboute membres vpon heed grete frontelet one holdynge myner ues tyme present stone perles jewelles ornementes verytable establysshed otherwyse vpon sholders hede yet sparpleth better fete rose place prudent oughte sapie vi et nono ecc xxvi uer ii well serue hym good herte bereth ye true swetnes dyuyne maieste lycour herbe ambrosia gyueth vnto tyme man refeccioned holdeth herte gyueth lyberte honour deiecteth grete synnes theyr good dedes remuneracyon yet neuer nyssheth hathe well done put place eternall whiche place shall mou te dapien viii uer vii uer iiii yf wyse dyscrete vnto lyfe eternall may well surmount tyrauntes whiche enemyes ye fayth realme haue hye kynge whiche may make v euer lyue go uerne temple haue fayth oure moder justice aunte bothe yonge olde hast come vnto pallas shall fynde none wery fountayne naturell refressheth humaynes wyse men hast kepe fayre mynerue hurte fooles wyll put sacke sholde grete shame reproche dyshonour vnto goddesse sholde seruytude foles seynge reuerenced amonge auncyent men wherfore payne defende certaynly ye bou de therto p concertacyon vertue voluptuosyte ca c x p ye whiche comysed beholde beholde frendes vertue surmysed voluptuosyte venyall thorughe demeanour bestyall wenynge oppresse whiche aboue empresse rede alchydes sawe dremynge two wayes whiche ryght dyfycyle behelde estate vtyle euyll gracyous vnderstondynge toke better waye moost iust waye moost surest waye myghte come consequently vnto mater purpose treate uoluptuosyte woman full worldly desyres solace joye pleasure aunte foule vayne donge whiche shall endure lytel whyle vertue wyl haue batayll agaynst voluptuosyte bothe bowes arowes puyssaunt dartes syege fayre saynges tulli whiche descended imperyal domynacyon al myghty god heuen uoluptuosyte loueth yonge chyldren vnberded mondaynes galautes holdeth loue estate pryncesse holdeth eternall sholde neuer haue ende woman fere thou lese thy soule fle carnalytees vyle dylectacyon taketh thy body grete vertues yf thou hole thy body macule thy brest yu adnychylleth thyn engyn brauches destroyeth also thy loyall thoughtes operacyons vycyous finis voluptatis mors est seneca vometh venym yonge folkes praye consyder present tyme fayre vertues doo venus may contrary embrasynge body fyre loue dampned p obieccyon voluptuosyte blamynge vertues ca c xi p grete enemye vertues loue nothynge warrynge grete maystry bycause luste wolde brynge whiche desyrynge gardyn full pleasaunce bothe synge daunce understonde scrypture voluptuosyte blameth vertues retayne well ye wordes ye shall newe thynges vertues propre enemye make esaie ii sapien ii hym mortall warre enuyroned pryncesse swete aurell odeferous herbes haue couertures sygne vyctorye tentes hanged therwith smell good oyntementes lycoures floures odeferous herbes clothes smelleth good odoures sylke bynde heere yelowe golde smelleth bawme bere large sleue grete rebrace halfe sleues cloth golde veluet galaunte haue smocke whyter crystal vestementes precyous resplendysshynge semely eyen caste pleasaunt lokes haue fayre hye forehede bere perles paste precyous stone jewel haue two chekes rede two rose lytell pappes made meruayllously haue yonge bachelers yt wyll breke theyr yongthe take dysportes mynyster vnto delytes honny take taken thoughtes wylles snare yf wyse sutyll holde besyde harpe lute melodyously sownynge sytte downe aboute mynyons syngynge dauncynge playnge balades roundelettes vyrelettes dytees musyke layes reioyce spyrytes haue fayre maydens besyde whyte smouthe remenaunte worlde make knyght shall haue labour peryll batayll shall fre entre maculed cryme yet shall deye certaynly shall fynde hymselfe bataylles fere stroke brusynges brekynge theyr harneys prynces present tyme sowne armye peasaunt syke wyll thynke euer vpon loue grete goddesse ye whiche dedes knowen thrugh worlde breste yssueth swete thynges pleasaunt cantycles playes j take jocundyte mondayne tyme presente promysed houre daye season whyle reason shall come aege dothe admonest youthe shall yssue v fayre dysportes beholde parys rauysshed fayre helayne bewaylynges gyuen vnto grekes haue made florysshe many sygnes dyuers countrees grete myghtye power haue pardoned good syth haue ben euyll cleopatra proude wyfe hathe serued lyberally cano pea also loued dylectacyon affryque put loue also well ammon dydde lyke wyse numyde maurisia athas honoured heuens thrughe regyons ynde delytes dy de please wonderfully wel sobrenes expulsed auncyentes hye phylosophers haue gretely honoured prayse decore appereth theyr good true scryptures absent ony body werke pleaseth hym v pleasaunce dylectacyons take pleasure ete reioyse v table lyues abredged warre yron soner laydein bedde accomplysshynge dylectacyon carnall dyuers kynges duke erles knyghtes haue done many valyaunces excellent prowess wonne many castelles townes cytees wherof haue ben cause haue vpon worlde domynacyon sardanapalus toke oure vestementes lefte royalles eccle xxxi rome tyme florysshed honoured aboue worlde dyde auauntage loued well hadde vertues scyence wysdome amonge v yonge folkes haue neuer colde alwayes junenalis oib terris naturall hete take reste dylectacyons fere set abacke v wherfore yonge lusty folkes loue soueraynly thynges delectables passe tyme olde folkes yt passeth aege vnderstonde well saynges reteyne theym within secretes youre hertes syth tyme dothe passe leseth day without takynge ony joy pleasure euery one loke reioyse drynkynge etynge euery repast delycate mete precyous loke whan sapien ecclesi x ye one passed pleasaunt worlde ye shall haue voluptuosyte pof answer vertue vnto voluptuosyte capitulo c xii po voluptuosyte wherfore doest thou put suche araye scossynge vengeable sore makynge grete fraye yet vyle beest thou saye thou arte transmutable unchaste abhomynable answer must vnto voluptuosyte ye whiche wyll excercyse batayl agaynst tell reason cause yu wylte assyste thou whiche arte prouoker eccle x vii capie vi baruth iii sorowe decepcyon thy myserable handes thou deceyueth yonge folkes wherfore praysest thou thy vyces lecheryes superfluous odour odorauntes ala thou knoweste well vaynglorye whiche endureth lytell whyle sobrenes thou arte enemye ebriete thou arte cosyn syster thy body full vycyousnes consyder well thou arte joly besemynge vn mondayne pleasure thou hast lace fayre gyrdylles hast thy heed thy body rychely aourned eyen tendre gracyous delectable swete fayre foreheed pleasaunt vysage thou hast resyste agaynste kepe thy poore lyfe thou wyit fyght agaynste harneys thou goost borowest whiche mauntell purple theresydue thy hole harneys stede baudryke thou werest clothe calmynye bereth male swerde salade spere instrument warre withoute armour body naked thou arte dyfycyle corrumpte thou takest worlde thy pleasure delycyous vanytees mondaynes besyde cupydo moder uenus whiche fyxed carnalytees cupydo virgilius plato alexander blynde ryght nature lytell stature holdynge bowe hande arowes dartes ye whiche casteth loue furyously arowes thou haste forged castynge thy ryght hande thou hast glasse whiche sheweth partyculerly thy superfluous euylles thy foreheed resteth lygh te grete noyses grete scandale lecherye al pryde hast shame wordes thy herte enpry ted vyle loue thyn eyen thy brest thy body juuenalis habandoned vnto myschefes thou makest noblenes come put dyscordes dyuerse place suffre grete extremytees epedymces bytter de thou makest sle sone bete fader yet dothe murdre peryssheth many men go vn heue myserye thou causeth grete maladyes wherof procedeth dethe lone whiche ha vnderstondynge pure clene thou hurteth hym vyllaynously chast hertes infeccyoned vnpropre many excellent vertues membres poore thou byndest dolour maketh ete mete tormente thy mouthe thou spekest golden wordes yong lynges thou makest incensyfes thy fylth impetuous dyminysseth dayes yf yonge berdles thou wolde rendre wt membres astonyed hora epi persius mylyon euylles thou enduceth take goodes folkes without ony hope euer make restytucyon amendes cofessyon someuer make worlde thou arte contrarye good condycyons dame reason neuer thy house dyscrecyon mynde wyll haue euyll tongue tryumphaunt folkes clerkes thou tornest vnto thy seruyce rede grete outrage tuli seneca epi noble dardamdes destroyed troye parthynyens dasie haue ben dystroyed thy luxuryosyte lyke wyse men actyque danayque cytees walles haue ben lost sodome tomorre haue ben foundred put bysmes wherof vale water excessyse full cruell destruccyon corynthes suffre theyr goodes house perysshed fayre realmes egypte surrye destroyed thou enten dest destroye rodyens myllenoys sybary en dyuers folkes thou wylte myne destroy thou pretendest abolysshe sobes tracyens pby thy false speche thou wylte corrumpe flaundres thou wylte domyne fraunce whiche doubte ouidius juuenalis grete euyll nacyons specyfyed haue ben punysshed thy carnall voluptuosyte happy lyfe perdurable heuens appertayneth worlde ye whiche transytorye pretende make good put ye waye lyfe conuaye ye porte salute gate heuen open vnto recupered meanes open vnto ye deedly synners whan drawe vnto buxumly hercules surmounted naturell enemye make establysshed persius boetius oui epist hye god one honoureth prayseth heuens lowly subdued ye al worlde yssueth al grete laudes honour salute reioyse vnder stondynge scyence hyghe feates dyuyne yelde subgectes instrued thou art replete wfylthe thou haste lechery without ony wyll eschewe prouoketh euery body lyue yu doest thy mouthe procedeth euyll haboundeth rychesse amyte iuste pyte good cou sayll glorye house chaste haue dwellynge worlde heuen myn onely habytacyon uer viii sapien iiii uer ix labour mounteth reason thyne holde vertues thou voluptuosyte thou louest yonge olde thou wolde haue honour bere sygne goddesse thou shalt grete pryncesse heuen yf thou wolde behoueth haue thy wyll corrupte take joyous remedye whiche enbraceth herte dyuyne vertues grete payne chauged ioy aboue hygh heuens shall mounte thou shall reste without ende fynally uertues dothe iuste warres enduceth ye londes gouerneth uer viii worlde contynually deuyseth bounte hys pleasure playes haue myn habandon whan seruynge vnto yonge folkes put vanyte plautus amphi uer vii loue well saynges holde blame yf contynue seruyce expulse vy ce fylthes bodyes yf fele fylthe wolde witholde come vnto flee dampnable synne take vertues clothe wt doctrynes techynges sauour ceasons shal haue true fayth seynge myghty stocke fooles peruers whiche grete flocke fooles renne vnto ryuage auaunce yourselfe hastely come fooles whiche blame renne vnto shyppe socyale ii q multi ec xiii et vii job xxx e v good operacyons erreth vpon see prouffyteth thynge vnto beware neptunus engloute youre shyppes insacyable wombe perysshed euermore neptunus p shyppe socyale mecanycque ca c xiiii p urbe men full excellente werke nothynge ne gardyse dyspende ony thynge ende dothe nothynge ought worthe selleth grete pryse good thynge halfe money destroyeth hymselfe gothe selleth noughty thynge moche money whiche er hathe grete losse hathe redy marchaudyse ezech vii whiche brade selleth good ware swereth affermeth good hondreth tymes poore foole thynkest thou god knoweth whiche thou doest rede nygardes ende uer xxvii may gadre rychesse wyll bye good che pe sell dere draper haue theyr house obscure derke ende euery clothe seme fyne begyn make theyr helles within theyr shoppes cogitatioes hoim oipoteti neq unt occultari xii c tua de symonia extra derke enuyous one vpon ye blamynge one auaryce desyre wynnynge grete payne maye one fynde one true marchaunt yf se true marchaunt ye whiche selleth good marchaundyse folysshe marchauntes shall blame hym bycause sholde haue good name euyll renowne wenynge drawe vnto good name p syngularyte newe fooles capitulo c xv p bycause sholde besy shyppe ferre nere take fooles whiche asprely brynge theyr gere thynkynge v go fere helpe v gouerne bothe purse sterne forgete rede scryptures newe fooles ye shall se thynges ryght necessary thoughte daye cleme ad nostrum de hereticis grete multytude fooles sholde come vnto shyppes begared thyrde ordre begyns well men woman full ypocrysye sye bycause shyppe lytell narowe put vndyscrete men muste make lyburne passe nacyons realmes countrees come begynde fooles sayd make spyrytes goo thynke man beynge worlde vertuous perfyte well man souerayne flesshe may ye moost excellentest place yf entached cryme synne euer prouffyteth happyer dedes wordes notwithstondynge theyr perfeccyon shyppe abydeth wandryn ge men renagates subtyll men hye shyppe goynge se ypocrytes wherfore folowe go theder ende multytude go without se se grete whiche hol deth many shyppes socoure yf encombred make deye leest entende vnto ende gyue vnto men vnderstonde deed yt theyr houre comen laboure eteth theym elles ordeyne gyue naturall gyfte whiche haue vowed close euery bodyes eyen foles grete daunger wyl knowe werke ye put rule vnto depryued lyghte strongely enclyned put waye also well contente honoure haue done seynge haue put comy shyppe carbases sadeled lyke consules se vyuyfyed folysshe folke ye shall theyr bende ye leest yf noted cryme euyll fame vpon erthe ye amonge ye wyse men shall auautages expulsed grete noyse bycause bere fruyte bycause wylnot people plebe gouernour relygyon clerkes preestes monkes cal haue nyce cogytacyons ye whiche dyspensed vse youre feates interdyted clementia de religiosis bus di clementi ad uostram euen nayans credo ye wysemen worthy shyppe false relygyon breweth grete sauce venym alemayne scintulle theutonique pullule moche grete rygour secte hathe grete puyssaunce p loyal frendes ende enfecte spyrytes parauenture ye myghte vnderstonde wolde saye euyll testefye neuer enuye speke euyll whiche haue taken cumentes holy faders ihesu cryste ought honoured excellence turbe vndyscrete wyll haue pacyence lerne nothynge demaudeth haue habyte vestement bewrappeth hym dole vnhappynes wyll laboure offyce win lyuynge angrye hym wyl haue vayne protestatio nihil dicere voluntas co tra bonos aut approbatos repos hathe one good purpose watche one houre daye laboure hathe ye wyl mary maudeleyne haue condycyons buffons full slouthe fere season begynde foles haue comytted dyuers euyls thrughe slouthe well lyeth erthe without hatayll euyll condycyons thynke euery thynge well ought dyspraysed thess ii honoured poynt counterfet saynge waye approued holy ghoost kepte full derely johanis iii onscientia plus fama romayns borne senatours full prudence haue ben swetely nourysshed entreated ye cradell without cyte lyue wel comaundementes lyue honestly without crysten people thou maye well bere armes make batayll sholde necessarye go agaynst infydeles nourysshe warre amonge crysten people thou gyueth many dyspences thou knoweth well ye woundynge ryght also ryght thou arte lorde mayster almoost worlde thou ought defende ryght mere ad imperatore iusti phe ony lyue yu smytest hym thyn vpon body grete horrour thou maynteynest warre agaynst crysten men otherwyse aduocates ought desyre principio de aduoca di uer udi comune welthe defende ryght equypared knyghtes knyghtes ly patrymony defended offyce necessary louable wherfore leue decepcyons false lagacyons maynteyne ryght put sergeauntes gode lyues offyces kepe people better puttynge grete sorte rascalles rybaudes pylleth poore people renneth nyght daye ye bordell vsurpynge euery body bycause bere name sergeauntes yf happen debate ony place theyr handes greced wyl let malefactours go yf haue comyssyon take ony body shall drynke hym payenge scotte wyll let hym go put good men offyce sholde nourysshynge ryght yf wyl lyue well dethe ye knowe houre shall deye dethe seketh eurous fleeth myserables p thynges contrary ca c xvii p whiche dothe contrary reason ryght equyte euer vary lyuynge grete perplexyte foole certaynte saynge scrypture lyueth well heuen sure haue spoken dyuers fooles whiche inordinato causa fueri destructionis oim rum oia q celo aut terris equore viuut ordine serua tur quem si destituant si ordine viuere cessent centinuo ite erunt nihilum que ruunt ni element ordine firmo starent statim iret profoundyte shyppe wyl speke thynges contrary haue theyr thoughtes dysordynate thynge cause dystruccyon thynges se dyuers trauersynge se without ore sayle without lawe without ordre whiche passynge haue recountred perylles mareswyne knowe seylla syrtes carybdim whiche perylles haue put haue ben swalowed suffred inestymable tormentes fynde folkes fooles syth theyr neyssaunce dyuers haue perysshed maner whiche haue transgressed lawe waye god hath determyned thynges thynges yt heuen erth see lyueth kepynge theyr ordre kepeth strongely vygoure whiche yf fayle cease theyr ordre incontynent theyr vertue shal passe fall vnto nought grete ruyne foles astonyed let iob xxxviii indicum v ordinatione tua perseuerant dy de pe dist ii hinc etiam lucifer adam layn abel gen iiii e doctryne thynges contrary knoweth well ynoughe euyl fere ye punycyon god knowe lucyfer felowes fell abysmes helle bycause kepte none ordre wolde contrary adam lyke wyse bycause none ordre case dyde contrary goddes comaundement felle pyteous ruyne cayn also bycause kepte none ordre dedes knewe well dyde euyll e broder abel made pyteous ende yf eleme te helde fixed theyr ordre sholde perysshe al sodaynly ala ought well drede whan thynges haue noo reason daunger punycyon thynges haue ordre certayne tyme space bere lyue deye vertue ord e kepe certayne lawe comaundementes ordeyned lytell ought obserue obeye greter tyme contrary done almoost thynges done contrary wherfore yf kepe better ordre lyke punysshed eternally moder god vyrgyninuyolate whiche hathe borne fruyte lyfe yelde uer xiiii et xix job xii p xxxvi put entyerly thy sauegarde ye ende thou aduocate towarde thy swete sone defende folysshe company whiche haue regned ion ge tyme wherfore testef ye ye shall neuer retorne agayne sygne therof cast ho de babyll behynde ouer medyatry vnto thy sone wyll pardone gyue mercye p pallas thou mynerue thanke eloquence thou hast gyuen melodyes thou haste euer reioysed lyke wyse scyence thou hast endued moyenny ge whiche haue fynysshed boke p gloryous sterre see souereyne refuge synners aduocate gendre humayne houre present prosterne thyn ymage knee bowed vnto erthe naked heed joyned handes rendrynge grace vnto thou hast implored towarde verbe incarnate whiche thou haste borne thy wombe vyrgynall hathe nourysshed gyuen hym souke thy pappes vyrgynalles neuer trust moder god vyrgyn immaculate yet agayne beseche thou holde thy hande vpon suche wyse may ende dayes se estate refulgent soule may borne presented aungelles joye eternall fader sone ye holy ghost maye alwaye remayne ye place prepayred iuste pardon redeth boke yf fynde ony thynge wel fra
